 For this, whatsapp Forwarded Tag will appear in the top left corner
 jaahir he company kaa makasad logon ko ye bataanaa he ki ye massej zyada forverd kiya ja rahaa he
 So that users can check the fake content

 The central government said on Friday that despite the drought conditions and less rainfall in some states, this year is not a panic
 labalab bhare khadyann bhandar or chini ke stock ke saath vah sthiti kaa muqabla karne ko taiyaar he
 Inaugurating 'foodcon 2012', Minister of State for Food, KV Thomas said that last year the production of food grains and sugar had been higher than anticipated, leaving the government with suitable food stocks in the warehouses for the coming year
 unhone kaha, khadyann bhandar ke maamle main bharat sarkaar sabase badi stocist he
 The Food Corporation of India currently has a stock of 82 million tonnes of food grains, while the public distribution system requires only 50 million tonnes of food grains
 tippaniyan Thomas said that the government has a stock of rice for one year, while wheat reserves are enough for three years, so there is nothing to worry about
 haalanki, unhone subjiyon, falon, khaadya telon or daal dalhan jaisi anya aavashyak vastuon kii kami ke bare main chetaya
 He said that some of these are imported
 bhartiya mausam vibhaag ne monsoon kii barish main 22 pratishat kami kaa anumaan lagaaya he

 isaki naubat dikhaai de rahi he! In Kundra village of Hamirpur district of Bundelkhand region of Uttar Pradesh, only women play Holi
 yahaan purushon kaa holi khelnaa varjit he
 Interestingly, when the male community in the country and abroad is colored in color and enjoying it on the day of Holi, in this small village of Bundelkhand, all the men of the village on the day of Holi are in the fields or from some other work Go outside
 isse bhi dilachasp baat he ki aamtaur par bachche jahaan puure saal holi khilne ko bekaraar rahete hai or pichakaari se lekar rangon kii kharid karte hai, vahiin kundara gaanv ke bachche rangon ke parv ke din saaf-suthere kapade pahanakar gharon main hi rahete hai
 It seems like it is Diwali, not Holi
 gaanv kii mahilaayein is din puri tarah aaazaad rahati hai
 364 days of the year, women who live in the curtain in front of the elders of the village, they do not veil from anyone on the day of Holi
 gaanv ke log bataate hai ki holi ke din gaanv ke hi ram janaki mandir main puure gaanv kii mahilaayein ekatra hoti hai or phag gane ke baad dhoomdhaam se holi khelti hai
 Dilawar Singh, Ramdin Meshram and Vivek Thakur said that several decades ago, on the very day of Holi, the villagers were singing in the Ramjanaki temple, when a prominent dacoit member, Member Singh, shot and killed Rajpal
 is ghatana ke baad is gaanv main kai saalon tak holi nahin manaai gai
 For a few years the women kept quiet, then they tried to convince the men and when they did not agree, all the women of the village gathered in the same Ram Janaki temple and decided that all the women of the village would celebrate the festival on Holi day with full rituals
 
 isamen purushon kii koi bhagidaar nahin rahegi
 The comments tabhi se gaanv main sirf mahilaayein holi khelti hai, mard hissaa nahin lete
 a lot of time has passed, but this is probably the only unique village where only women power enjoys playing Holi

 Even more interesting is that generally, where children are eager to play Holi throughout the year and buy colors ranging from the pitch, the children of Kundra village stay in homes wearing clean clothes on the day of colors
 aisa lagata he, maano holi nahin, diwali ho

 bhagwaan ram ne ravan kaa vadh kiya tha or isiilie dashahra kaa tyohaar manaaya jaataa he
 But this is the fact that we all know
 lekin dashahra ke bare main ham yahaan kuch aise tathy bataa rahe hai, jise shaayad hi aap jaanate hon
 
 
 1
 dashahrasanskrit shabd dasha or haara se bana he
 Which simply means the defeat of the sun
 kaha jaataa he ki agar ravan kaa vadh bhagwaan ram ne nahin kiya hota to surya hameshaa ke liye ast ho jaataa
 2
 dashahra ko vijaydashmike naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 Which means the victory on the tenth day
 iskaa mahatv is rup main bhi hota ki maa durga ne dasven din mahisasur rakshas kaa vadh kiya tha
 3
 mahisasur asuron ko raja tha, jo bhole-bhaale logon par atyaachaar karata tha
 Seeing his atrocities, Lord Brahma, Vishnu and Mahesh created power
 mahisasur or shakti ke bich 10 dinon tak yuddh hua or aakhirkaar maa ne 10wein din vijay hasil kar lee
 4
 aisi manyata he ki navaratri main maa apane maayke aati hai or dasven din unki vidaai hoti he
 This is the reason why on the tenth day of Loganavratri immerse them in water
 5
 There is also a belief that Rama slaughtered Ravana's ten heads, which is seen to symbolically link the elimination of the 10 evils within him
 paap, kaam, krodh, moh, lobh, ghamand, swaarth, jalan, ahankaar, amaanavtaa or anyaay wo das buraaiyaan hai
 6
 aisa kaha jaataa he ki pehali baar dashahra mysore ke raja ke raaj main 17veen shatabdi main manaai gai thi,7
 This festival is celebrated not only in India but also in Bangladesh and Nepal
 malaysia main dashahra par rashtriya avkaash hota
 8
 dashahra tyoharko mausam badalane se jodakar bhi dekha jaataa he
 Dussehra begins with winter
 yah kharif kii kheti kaa mausam bhi hota he
 Kharif is harvested and Rabi sowing begins after Diwali
 9
 Dussehra signifies the importance of both Lord Rama and Mother Durga
 ravan ko haraane ke liye shri ram ne maa durga kii puja kii thi or arshivaad ke rup main maa ne ravan ko maarane kaa rahasy bataaya tha
 10
 ek or manyata yah he ki dashahra ke din hi raja ashok ne buddha dharm apanaaya tha
 On this day, Dr
 ambedkar ne bhi buddha dharm apanaaya tha
